# 진범 찾기 원문 로그

**Gamemaster:** 이브의 부탁으로 호위를 찾아온 일행.
그러나 누명을 쓴 채였고, 누명을 벗기려면 확실한 증거가 필요한 상황.

**Gamemaster:** 지난 밤, 일행은 보안관을 설득하여 추가로 조사할 시간을 손에 넣었습니다.

**Gamemaster:** 일행은 처형시간 전부터 보안관저에 모여 있습니다.

**보안관:** 보안관이 처형 시간이 되어 몰려든 사람들을 진정시키려고 애쓰고 있군요.

**민간인 남성:** 밖에서는 거친 목소리들이 들려옵니다.

**민간인 남성:** “일주일? 그 살인자를 일주일이나 더 먹여 살리겠단 말이오?”

**민간인 여성:** “사제님은 이미 땅에 묻혔는데, 왜 저 쓰레기는 아직 살아 있는거에요!”

**매그너스:** (요오시 즉 전원 몰살..!

**민간인 남성:** "죽여라! 죽여라!"

**엘테라 마스테:** @밖에 비가 오는걸 보고 창문을 멍하니 바라보다가 주민들의 목소리들을 듣자 본인 마음에 안 드는지 인상을 씁니다

**네모(Nemo):** (일단 저는 전과 같이 오크 상태입니다)

**헤카트리엘:** @소곤소곤 "저러고 있는 걸 보면 다 죽여버리고 싶단 말이야, 시체인 때가 더 쓸모있겠어."

**엘테라 마스테:** @헤카트에게 "…그래도 이성은 놓지 말아주세요 그 녀석처럼요"

**매그너스:** "솔직히 나도 절반쯤 동의해"

**보안관:** 보안관은 병사들을 이용해 군중을 물립니다만, 병사들 또한 그 명령이 달갑지 않아보이는군요.

**헤카트리엘:** "그러엄, 일은 일이니까."

**카린츠:** 노숙을 마치고 먼지투성이 모습으로 군중들 틈에서 걸어나옵니다

**카린츠:** 그러다가 병사들 사이로 가서 몸으로 밀치면서 "…관계자야." 하고 들어섭니다

**엘테라 마스테:** (비 맞고 있었니…?

**보안관:** "카린츠 자네도 왔군. 들어가게."

**카린츠:** 들어와서 일행을 보더니

**네모(Nemo):** (네모는 지금 오크 상태이기 때문에 우선 반란분자 등이 있는지 확인하면서 멀리 있습니다

**카린츠:** 잠시 비스듬히 시선을 내리며 머리를 긁적거립니다

**카린츠:** "있잖아. 자면서 생각해봤는데…"

**카린츠:** "…다시 생각해도 내가 잘못한 건 없는거 같은데……" 하면서 기죽은 기색으로 말합니다

**엘테라 마스테:** "새벽에 여관으로 들어올 줄 알았는데…끝까지 거기에 있을줄은 몰랐는데…"

**엘테라 마스테:** "…네가 어제부터 계속 같은 말을 하면 우리도 같은 말을 내뱉을 뿐이야"

**카구야:** @흘깃 보고는 "…켁. 용캐도 다시 오시는군요. 질리지도 않으시나요?"

**엘테라 마스테:** "그런 생각이 여전히 있다면…왜 돌아온거야?"

**카린츠:** "…… 그렇더라도."

**헤카트리엘:** "우리가 암살이나 섬멸 의뢰를 받은 거라면 네가 잘못한 게 하등 없거든, 그런 일이 아니니까 그렇지."

**카린츠:** "자주 마주치는 사이에 미움받고 싶지는 않으니까…"

**카린츠:** "일단은 협력… 이라고나 할까. 음… 그러니까."

**카린츠:** "괜찮겠지?"

**엘테라 마스테:** "마주쳤지…자주…."

**엘테라 마스테:** "그럼 네가 이브 씨에게 준 종이. 우리에게도 줘."

**헤카트리엘:** "응? 각서 같은 거야?"

**네모(Nemo):** (혹시 많은 인파를 바라봤을 때, 군중 속에 섞인 이상한 사람은 없는거죠?

**카린츠:** "그건… 강제력이 없어… 그러니까 무녀한테는 내가 자의로 간거라고 해야하나. 자원봉사 같은 느낌으로…"

**카구야:** "싫어요. 당신같은 사람. 있어봤자 또 문제만… 네!?" @엘테라의 말을 듣고 말을 멈춥니다.

**보안관:** 그런 사람은 보이지 않는군요.

**카린츠:** "통제 반지는 교단에서 지정한 의뢰인에게 주어지는거야. 저번… 마키나 토벌전 처럼."

**헤카트리엘:** "자원봉사로 친구 죽이기?"

**엘테라 마스테:** "…그럼 반지는?"

**헤카트리엘:** "그냥… 하고 싶어서 저질렀다 그래."

**네모(Nemo):** (군중 속에서 이상한 사람은 없다는 것을 확인하고 일행들과 합류합니다)"다행히 선동가나 이런 자들은 없는것 같군"

**카린츠:** "그러니까 이건 교단에서 지정한 임무가 아니고 내 자의적으로 무녀를 도우려고 왔던거지."

**헤카트리엘:** "그러면 도움이 우선이지, 네 정의가 우선이야? 뭐, 이미 저지른 뒤니까 더 뭐라고는 안 할게."

**엘테라 마스테:** "…벌 받는 자 치고는 팔자 좋은걸…그럼 우리가 이번에 추적 할 자를 네가 또 죽일 때도 같은 일을 또 보라는건 아니겠지…?"

**카린츠:** "하지만 무녀의 호위병이… 저주받은 무기를 쓰는 이 임무에 임하면서 알게된 정보야."

**카린츠:** "난 너희가 무녀의 부탁이란 이유로 모든걸 다 뒤로 미루어놓는 이유가 뭔지 모르겠어."

**매그너스:** "응?"

**카린츠:** "만약… 저기 갇힌 녀석이 언데드를 부리는 강령술사라면 너희는 그래도 여전히 그를 구할거야?"

**헤카트리엘:** "그럴건데?"

**매그너스:** "자기 마음에 안들면 다 쳐죽여버리는게"

**매그너스:** "맞다는건가ㅣ?"

**매그너스:** "일단 할건 하고 쳐죽여야지"

**카구야:** (이 세계의 강령술은 허가되어있다

**엘테라 마스테:** "…이미 영혼부터 계약한 시점에서 언데드야…그런 논리는 내게 안 통할걸"

**매그너스:** "의뢰주님이 우리 뒤통수를 친것도 아니고"

**네모(Nemo):** "우선 살려야 할 사람은 살려야 할 것 아닙니까 카린츠 씨."

**카구야:** (라고 들었다

**헤카트리엘:** "내가 그랬잖아, 다 끝나면 네가 따로 처죽여도 안 막아."

**헤카트리엘:** "근데 네가 우리랑 한 배에 탄 이상, 네가 지금 처죽이면 우리가 죽인 거야."

**헤카트리엘:** "우리가 죽이고 싶든 아니든."

**카구야:** "봐요. 다 알고도 자기 생각만 한거라구요. 이래도 같이 다닐거에요?" @옆에 있는 사람들에게

**엘테라 마스테:** "…"

**카린츠:** "어차피 나중에 처단해도 된다면 지금 하면 안될 이유는 뭐야? 너희가 죽인 것처럼 된다는 그런… 인식 자체 때문인가."

**매그너스:** "하아.."

**카린츠:** "임무 성공이란 딱지때문에?"

**헤카트리엘:** "너, 지금 그냥 자의로 온 거지? 무녀의 부탁따위 안 듣고 온 거지?"

**헤카트리엘:** "제발 좀 굽힐 줄 알라고, 일이란 걸 하겠다면."

**엘테라 마스테:** "무녀의 부탁으로 왔다면서…죽이는건 자기 마음대로라. 웃기지도 않는걸"

**헤카트리엘:** "그게 싫으면 네가 독자적 행동을 벌이라고."

**카린츠:** "오해하지마. 나도 처음에는… 오로지 호의… 그리고 내 자의적으로 선행을 했다는 딱지 하나를 얻고 싶어서 무녀에게 협력하기로 한거야."

**매그너스:** "내가 보기엔 저 녀석 그냥 사람 죽이는걸 좋아하는것같은데"

**네모(Nemo):** "우선 차근차근 해결해 나가야 하니까요. 지금 그런 것은 나중에 치우고 우선 지금 앞에 닥친 일을 해결하자고요"

**매그너스:** "그냥 죽이게 내버려두지?"

**매그너스:** "저런 타입은, 나중에 자기가 했던대로 똑같이 뒤에서 칼맞아 죽는 타입이니까"

**엘테라 마스테:** "…지금은 이 일의 주동자를 찾는 것부터 해야겠어요"

**카린츠:** "난… 살인귀 같은게 아닌데…" 눈동자가 억울함으로 가라앉습니다

**보안관:** "잘 말해주었군 네모."

**매그너스:** "응?"

**보안관:** 보안관이 외부의 소란이 진정되자 따라 들어옵니다.

**매그너스:** "뭔 헛소리지?"

**헤카트리엘:** "지대하게 착각하는 모양인데, 어차피 할 것을 지금 안 하는 건 하겠다는 의지를 져버리는 게 아니라고?"

**매그너스:** "살인귀 맞잖아"

**매그너스:** "아니지, 그냥 살인중독자지"

**매그너스:** "즐겁지?"

**헤카트리엘:** "네가 발 뒤로 몇번 걸었다고 후퇴가 아니야, 이 사람아."

**매그너스:** "저자는 악인이다 그러니 내가 죽인다"

**매그너스:** "캬! 나 멋지다!"

**보안관:** "자네들, 이제는 밖에 사람들로 모자라서 자네들까지 내 속을 썩이려는 건가?"

**매그너스:** "악을 처단하는 내 멋짐에 취한다!"

**매그너스:** "이거잖아"

**엘테라 마스테:** "…저기, 보안관 씨"

**매그너스:** "츠하하하하!"

**카린츠:** "…그렇게 날 한껏 비아냥 거려도 내가 널 쳐죽이지 않는 것이 내가 살인귀가 아니란 증거야."

**카린츠:** 으르렁 거리며 말합니다

**헤카트리엘:** "살인귀는 죽일 때를 아는데?"

**엘테라 마스테:** "주민들 얘기 중에 식량 얘기를 들었는데…묘하게 신경 쓰이네요. 그것마저도 눈치를 봐야 하는 상황인가요…?"

**보안관:** "왜 그러지?"

**매그너스:** "설마, 네가 날 안죽이는건, 내가 네 기준 살인 조건을 충족하지 않았기대문이지"

**보안관:** "그렇지 않네. 그냥… 하는 소리지."

**헤카트리엘:** "그냥 꼴같잖다고 칼 들이대는 건 꼰대잖아."

**네모(Nemo):** "다른 것들은 다 집어 치우고 지금 해야할 것에 집중하시죠."

**보안관:** "먹일 음식도 아깝다는 상투적인 소리 아니겠나."

**카린츠:** "그럼 지금부터는 뭘 해야해?"

**엘테라 마스테:** "…그건 다행이네요…그럼 네모 씨"

**엘테라 마스테:** "어제 발견한 장부…우리에게 다시 보여줘서 정리 하는 것부터 해볼까요"

**보안관:** "자네들이 가져온 가짜 장부랑 수레에 실려있던 물자들은 새벽에 옮겨왔네."

**헤카트리엘:** "잘 들어봐, 네가 지금 치지 않는 건 당장 죽여봤자 뿌리 끝만 회치는 것이기 때문이야."

**헤카트리엘:** "너는 기다릴 줄 알아야 하고, 그것이 진짜 악의 뿌리를 치는 것임을 상기해야 해."

**카구야:** @무어라 말하려다가 보안관을 보고 말을 삼킵니다.

**헤카트리엘:** "살인기술밖에 모른다면 말이야."

**카린츠:** "……"

**보안관:** "이것들을 조사한 결과, 대부분은 어디서나 볼법한 물건이지만 딱 한 상자에 아우렐리아 항구의 직인이 찍혀있음이 밝혀졌지."

**엘테라 마스테:** "…항구…요?"

**네모(Nemo):** "저희가 가야 합니까?"

**보안관:** "그렇네. 이곳에서 편도로 사흘 정도 걸리는 곳이지."

**매그너스:** "아하, 생각해보니 저주를 쓴다는 저자는 무녀의 수하지?"

**매그너스:** "그럼 무녀까지 쳐죽여야겠군"

**헤카트리엘:** "본능밖에 모를 줄로 보이는 짐승들도, 무턱대고 죽여 먹는 게 전부가 아니야."

**매그너스:** "오, 그 다음은 또 누구를 죽일까? 무녀를 키워낸사람들?"

**매그너스:** "그 다음은 또 누구? 오… 멋진걸"

**헤카트리엘:** "살수면 포식자답게 굴어, 사냥감처럼 마구 날뛰지 말고."

**매그너스:** "세계수 슬레이어라"

**보안관:** "내가 직접 조사하러 갈 수도 있지만 그랬다가 성난 군중이 화를 일으킬까 두렵군."

**카린츠:** 쏟아지는 비난과 비판에 입을 꾹 다물고 있다가

**엘테라 마스테:** "사흘….조사가 일주일 정도라면 아무리 빨리 가서 반나절 정도의 여유 밖에 없을텐데…혹시 그 직인, 정확히 어디인지 볼 수 있을까요?"

**카린츠:** "있잖아…? 어제 내가 자면서 생각한건 또 하나가 있긴한데."

**카린츠:** "살해당했다는 사제는 위그드라실의 축복과 무관한 사람이야?"

**엘테라 마스테:** @직인을 봅니다. 적어도 어디에서 배송 했는지에 대한것인지

**카구야:** "여러분? 보는 눈이 있사와요. 가끔은 혀를 쉬게 두는 게 어떠신지?" @매그너스에게 눈짓

**매그너스:** 카구야를 보며 말합니다.

**매그너스:** "츠하하하하핫!"

**보안관:** "축복과는 무관하지만, 세계수와 관련이 없다고 할 순 없지."

**보안관:** "연맹에서 파견된 자니까."

**보안관:** "그리고 상자의 직인은 아우렐리아 항구의 세관을 통과할때 찍히는 직인일세."

**매그너스:** "말 해야할때를 모르면 안하는것만 모르니, 해야할 말을 모르는 너도 침묵이 맞을걸?"

**카린츠:** "그러면 보안관. 그 세계수 사냥꾼들에게도 사제를 살해할 동기가 있는거 아니야?"

**엘테라 마스테:** @손으로 이마를 짚고는 "…"

**보안관:** "그렇지."

**카린츠:** "그러면 그들의 존재를 확실하게 증명할 수 있으면 되겠네."

**보안관:** "평범한 사람들은 눈앞에 있는 증거를 들이밀길 원하네."

**보안관:** 카린츠의 말에 끄덕입니다

**카린츠:** "하지만 상인을 포함한 저 수많은 시체들로도 증명이 안된다면 더 핵심적인 증거가 필요하단 뜻이겠구나."

**보안관:** "적어도 그들이 했다는 확실한 증거만 있다면…"

**네모(Nemo):** (이 세계에 카메라와 비슷한 거는 없겠죠?

**보안관:** (없겠군요.

**엘테라 마스테:** "지금은 아우렐리아 항구로 가보는걸로 해요"

**보안관:** "수레에 실린만큼의 물건이 모두 아우렐리아 항구에서 나왔다면, 필시 그곳에 놈들의 기지가 있을걸세."

**엘테라 마스테:** "아마 그들의 성향이라면 대놓고 움직일 가능성이 많아요…숨어 있어도 우리에게 어차피 다가 올테구요"

**네모(Nemo):** "걸어서 3일 걸린다고 하지 않았나?"

**보안관:** "본래 사제를 죽이기 위해 마을에 접근했다면 그에 관한 자료도 있을 터…"

**헤카트리엘:** "운전해 줘?"

**카린츠:** "일리 있어. 예전에 에드릭 벨몬드도 배로 물건을 옮겼거든… 그것이 물건이든 사람이든."

**엘테라 마스테:** "조사에는 일주일…즉, 지금이라도 안가면 시간은 더 촉박해질거에요."

**Gamemaster:** 아우렐리아 항구는 입구에 들어서기 전부터 소란스럽습니다.

You touch a willing creature who isn’t wearing armor. Until the spell ends, the target’s base AC becomes 13 plus its Dexterity modifier. The spell ends early if the target dons armor.

**카구야:** @걸어가면서 작은 목소리로 주문

**카구야:** Illusory Instrument 환영계
You create an illusionary copy of a mundane musical instrument. The copy of the instrument takes on the shape of your fondest memory of the instrument, such as the first flute you owned or the half harp gifted to you by a loved one. This illusion moves as its physical counterpart would, but it is weightless and is tangible only to you. This instrument can be used as a Spellcasting Focus. This illusory instrument dissipates if you move 10 feet away from it or choose to end the spell (no action required by you). As a Bonus Action, you can command your instrument to create one of the following effects: Mimic basic sounds heard on a daily basis, such as a bird chirping, footsteps, or a slamming door. Automatically play a basic beat at the tempo of your choice. Record anything played on it, and play it back on a loop. Record and playback any noise that it could pick up within 15 feet, such as conversation, a royal decree, or a snoring party member who swears that they don’t snore.
음 및 동 Action 10분 접촉

**매그너스:** Rage Feature
You can imbue yourself with a primal power called Rage, a force that grants you extraordinary might and resilience. You can enter it as a Bonus Action if you aren’t wearing Heavy armor. You can enter your Rage the number of times shown for your Barbarian level in the Rages column of the Barbarian Features table. You regain one expended use when you finish a Short Rest, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. While active, your Rage follows the rules below. Damage Resistance. You have Resistance to Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing damage. Rage Damage. When you make an attack using Strength—with either a weapon or an Unarmed Strike—and deal damage to the target, you gain a bonus to the damage that increases as you gain levels as a Barbarian, as shown in the Rage Damage column of the Barbarian Features table. Strength Advantage. You have Advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. No Concentration or Spells. You can’t maintain Concentration, and you can’t cast spells. Duration. The Rage lasts until the end of your next turn, and it ends early if you don Heavy armor or have the Incapacitated condition. If your Rage is still active on your next turn, you can extend the Rage for another round by doing one of the following: Make an attack roll against an enemy. Force an enemy to make a saving throw. Take a Bonus Action to extend your Rage. Each time the Rage is extended, it lasts until the end of your next turn. You can maintain a Rage for up to 10 minutes.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Bonus Action 10 minutes Self Self

**헤카트리엘:** Bardic Inspiration Feature
You can supernaturally inspire others through words, music, or dance. This inspiration is represented by your Bardic Inspiration die, which is a d6. Using Bardic Inspiration. As a Bonus Action, you can inspire another creature within 60 feet of yourself who can see or hear you. That creature gains one of your Bardic Inspiration dice. A creature can have only one Bardic Inspiration die at a time. Once within the next hour when the creature fails a D20 Test, the creature can roll the Bardic Inspiration die and add the number rolled to the d20, potentially turning the failure into a success. A Bardic Inspiration die is expended when it’s rolled. Number of Uses. You can confer a Bardic Inspiration die a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier (minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. At Higher Levels. Your Bardic Inspiration die changes when you reach certain Bard levels, as shown in the Bardic Die column of the Bard Features table. The die becomes a d8 at level 5, a d10 at level 10, and a d12 at level 15.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Action 1 hour 60 ft 1 creature

**엘테라 마스테:** Mirror Image 3rd Level • Illusion
Three illusory duplicates of yourself appear in your space. Until the spell ends, the duplicates move with you and mimic your actions, shifting position so it’s impossible to track which image is real. Each time a creature hits you with an attack roll during the spell’s duration, roll a d6 for each of your remaining duplicates. If any of the d6s rolls a 3 or higher, one of the duplicates is hit instead of you, and the duplicate is destroyed. The duplicates otherwise ignore all other damage and effects. The spell ends when all three duplicates are destroyed. A creature is unaffected by this spell if it has the Blinded condition, Blindsight, or Truesight.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
V, S Action 1 minute Self Self

**카린츠:** Vow of Enmity Feature
When you take the Attack action, you can expend one use of your Channel Divinity to utter a vow of enmity against a creature you can see within 30 feet of yourself. You have Advantage on attack rolls against the creature for 1 minute or until you use this feature again. If the creature drops to 0 Hit Points before the vow ends, you can transfer the vow to a different creature within 30 feet of yourself (no action required).

This bow has multiple strings and resembles a lyre or small harp. By strumming the strings while setting an arrow to the bow, you imbue the arrow with magic. You can play one of the following melodies when you use the bow to make a ranged weapon attack. You must choose to do so before you make the attack roll, and you can play only one melody per attack. Melody of Precision. If you’re proficient in Performance, you gain a +1 bonus to the attack roll. If you have expertise in Performance, you gain a +2 bonus instead. Melody of Reverberation. The melody you strum echoes loudly. On a hit, the target takes extra thunder damage equal to your Charisma modifier.

**카구야:** Bardic Inspiration 특성
You can supernaturally inspire others through words, music, or dance. This inspiration is represented by your Bardic Inspiration die, which is a d6. Using Bardic Inspiration. As a Bonus Action, you can inspire another creature within 60 feet of yourself who can see or hear you. That creature gains one of your Bardic Inspiration dice. A creature can have only one Bardic Inspiration die at a time. Once within the next hour when the creature fails a D20 Test, the creature can roll the Bardic Inspiration die and add the number rolled to the d20, potentially turning the failure into a success. A Bardic Inspiration die is expended when it’s rolled. Number of Uses. You can confer a Bardic Inspiration die a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier (minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. At Higher Levels. Your Bardic Inspiration die changes when you reach certain Bard levels, as shown in the Bardic Die column of the Bard Features table. The die becomes a d8 at level 5, a d10 at level 10, and a d12 at level 15.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Action 1시간 60ft 1 creatures

**카구야:** Inspired Eclipse 특성
When you take a Bonus Action to give a creature a Bardic Inspiration die, you can have the Invisible condition and teleport up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space you can see as part of that Bonus Action. This invisibility lasts until the start of your next turn and ends early immediately after you make an attack roll, deal damage, or cast a spell.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Targets
카구야 카구야
Bonus Action 즉시 30ft Self

Pneumatic Strike. After you make an attack roll with this weapon, but before the result of the attack is determined, you can use a bonus action to pull the blade’s trigger. With a pneumatic thrust, the top of the weapon arcs forward and you gain a +4 bonus to the attack roll.
Tetanus Blade. When you hit a creature with an attack that uses Pneumatic Strike, the pathogens that live within the rusty blade are reinvigorated by its magic, and the attack deals an additional 4 (1d8) Poison damage.Backfire. When you roll an 8 on Tetanus Blade’s poison damage, dormant pathogens within surrounding creatures become reinvigorated. Each creature within 10 feet of you (including you) must succeed on a DC 15 Constitution saving throw or take 14 (4d6) Poison damage and become poisoned until the end of its next turn.

**헤카트리엘:** Hypnotic Pattern 3rd Level • Illusion
You create a twisting pattern of colors in a 30-foot Cube within range. The pattern appears for a moment and vanishes. Each creature in the area who can see the pattern must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or have the Charmed condition for the duration. While Charmed, the creature has the Incapacitated condition and a Speed of 0. The spell ends for an affected creature if it takes any damage or if someone else uses an action to shake the creature out of its stupor.

**매그너스:** Reckless Attack Feature
You can throw aside all concern for defense to attack with increased ferocity. When you make your first attack roll on your turn, you can decide to attack recklessly. Doing so gives you Advantage on attack rolls using Strength until the start of your next turn, but attack rolls against you have Advantage during that time.

**네모(Nemo):** Justice 발동!
당신은 잠시 운명의 저울추를 맞출 수 있는 능력을 얻습니다. 앞으로 8시간 동안, 당신 또는 당신으로부터 60피트 이내에 있는 생명체가 이점 또는 불이익을 적용하여 d20 주사위를 굴리려고 할 때마다, 당신은 반응 행동을 사용하여 해당 주사위 굴림이 이점 또는 불이익의 영향을 받지 않도록 할 수 있습니다.
적군이 유리점을 굴릴 시, 유리점 제거
아군이 불리점을 굴릴 시, 불리점 제거

**네모(Nemo):** Chaos Bolt 1st Level • Evocation
You hurl an undulating, warbling mass of chaotic energy at one creature in range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 2d8 + 1d6 damage. Choose one of the d8s. The number rolled on that die determines the attack’s damage type, as shown below.
d8 Damage Type 1 Acid 2 Cold 3 Fire 4 Force 5 Lightning 6 Poison 7 Psychic 8 Thunder
Open RollTable Chaos Bolt: Damage Type
If you roll the same number on both d8s, the chaotic energy leaps from the target to a different creature of your choice within 30 feet of it. Make a new attack roll against the new target, and make a new damage roll, which could cause the chaotic energy to leap again. A creature can be targeted only once by each casting of this spell. At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 2nd level or higher, each target takes 1d6 extra damage of the type rolled for each slot level above 1st.

**네모(Nemo):** Lucky Origin Feat
Origin Feat You gain the following benefits. Luck Points. You have a number of Luck Points equal to your Proficiency Bonus and can spend the points on the benefits below. You regain your expended Luck Points when you finish a Long Rest. Advantage. When you roll a d20 for a D20 Test, you can spend 1 Luck Point to give yourself Advantage on the roll. Disadvantage. When a creature rolls a d20 for an attack roll against you, you can spend 1 Luck Point to impose Disadvantage on that roll.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Special Instantaneous Self 1 creature

**네모(Nemo):** Tides of Chaos Feature
You can manipulate chaos itself to give yourself Advantage on one D20 Test before you roll the d20. Once you do so, you must cast a Sorcerer spell with a spell slot or finish a Long Rest before you can use this feature again. If you do cast a Sorcerer spell with a spell slot before you finish a Long Rest, you automatically roll on the Wild Magic Surge table.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Special Instantaneous Self

**네모(Nemo):** Lucky Origin Feat
Origin Feat You gain the following benefits. Luck Points. You have a number of Luck Points equal to your Proficiency Bonus and can spend the points on the benefits below. You regain your expended Luck Points when you finish a Long Rest. Advantage. When you roll a d20 for a D20 Test, you can spend 1 Luck Point to give yourself Advantage on the roll. Disadvantage. When a creature rolls a d20 for an attack roll against you, you can spend 1 Luck Point to impose Disadvantage on that roll.

**엘테라 마스테:** Eye Burn Transmutation
You sting the eyes of a creature attacking you. The target must make a Constitution saving throw (a creature with Blindsight or Immunity to the Blinded condition succeeds automatically). On a failed save, the target has the Blinded condition until the end of the turn. On a successful save, it must subtract 1d4 from the triggering attack roll. The target automatically succeeds on its saves against your subsequent casting of this spell for 24 hours.

**카린츠:** Vow of Enmity Feature
When you take the Attack action, you can expend one use of your Channel Divinity to utter a vow of enmity against a creature you can see within 30 feet of yourself. You have Advantage on attack rolls against the creature for 1 minute or until you use this feature again. If the creature drops to 0 Hit Points before the vow ends, you can transfer the vow to a different creature within 30 feet of yourself (no action required).

Guided by a flash of magical insight, you make one attack with the weapon used in the spell’s casting. The attack uses your spellcasting ability for the attack and damage rolls instead of using Strength or Dexterity. If the attack deals damage, it can be Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type (your choice). Cantrip Upgrade. Whether you deal Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type, the attack deals extra Radiant damage when you reach levels 5 (1d6), 11 (2d6), and 17 (3d6).

**카구야:** Longbow of Melodies 군용 원거리 무기 • Slow
This bow has multiple strings and resembles a lyre or small harp. By strumming the strings while setting an arrow to the bow, you imbue the arrow with magic. You can play one of the following melodies when you use the bow to make a ranged weapon attack. You must choose to do so before you make the attack roll, and you can play only one melody per attack. Melody of Precision. If you’re proficient in Performance, you gain a +1 bonus to the attack roll. If you have expertise in Performance, you gain a +2 bonus instead. Melody of Reverberation. The melody you strum echoes loudly. On a hit, the target takes extra thunder damage equal to your Charisma modifier.

This spell accelerates or decelerates an attack (see the chosen effect below) the instant before it strikes, lessening or multiplying its force. Accelerate. The target takes an extra 2d6 damage from the attack. This extra damage is the same type dealt by the triggering attack. Decelerate. Reduce the damage the target takes by 2d6 (to a minimum of 0 damage). Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The extra damage or reduction in damage increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1.

Pneumatic Strike. After you make an attack roll with this weapon, but before the result of the attack is determined, you can use a bonus action to pull the blade’s trigger. With a pneumatic thrust, the top of the weapon arcs forward and you gain a +4 bonus to the attack roll.
Tetanus Blade. When you hit a creature with an attack that uses Pneumatic Strike, the pathogens that live within the rusty blade are reinvigorated by its magic, and the attack deals an additional 4 (1d8) Poison damage.Backfire. When you roll an 8 on Tetanus Blade’s poison damage, dormant pathogens within surrounding creatures become reinvigorated. Each creature within 10 feet of you (including you) must succeed on a DC 15 Constitution saving throw or take 14 (4d6) Poison damage and become poisoned until the end of its next turn.

You sting the eyes of a creature attacking you. The target must make a Constitution saving throw (a creature with Blindsight or Immunity to the Blinded condition succeeds automatically). **카구야:** Moon's Inspiration 특성
The primal and ever-changing power of the moon flows through you, granting you the following benefits.Inspired Eclipse. When you take a Bonus Action to give a creature a Bardic Inspiration die, you can have the Invisible condition and teleport up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space you can see as part of that Bonus Action. This invisibility lasts until the start of your next turn and ends early immediately after you make an attack roll, deal damage, or cast a spell.Lunar Vitality. Once per turn when you restore Hit Points to a creature with a spell, you can expend a Bardic Inspiration die and increase the amount of Hit Points restored by a number equal to a roll of the Bardic Inspiration die. The creature’s Speed also increases by 10 feet until the end of its next turn.

**카구야:** Bardic Inspiration 특성
You can supernaturally inspire others through words, music, or dance. This inspiration is represented by your Bardic Inspiration die, which is a d6. Using Bardic Inspiration. As a Bonus Action, you can inspire another creature within 60 feet of yourself who can see or hear you. That creature gains one of your Bardic Inspiration dice. A creature can have only one Bardic Inspiration die at a time. Once within the next hour when the creature fails a D20 Test, the creature can roll the Bardic Inspiration die and add the number rolled to the d20, potentially turning the failure into a success. A Bardic Inspiration die is expended when it’s rolled. Number of Uses. You can confer a Bardic Inspiration die a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier (minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. At Higher Levels. Your Bardic Inspiration die changes when you reach certain Bard levels, as shown in the Bardic Die column of the Bard Features table. The die becomes a d8 at level 5, a d10 at level 10, and a d12 at level 15.

**네모(Nemo):** Innate Sorcery Feature
An event in your past left an indelible mark on you, infusing you with simmering magic. As a Bonus Action, you can unleash that magic for 1 minute, during which you gain the following benefits: The spell save DC of your Sorcerer spells increases by 1. You have Advantage on the attack rolls of Sorcerer spells you cast. You can use this feature twice, and you regain all expended uses of it when you finish a Long Rest.

You can throw aside all concern for defense to attack with increased ferocity. When you make your first attack roll on your turn, you can decide to attack recklessly. Pneumatic Strike. After you make an attack roll with this weapon, but before the result of the attack is determined, you can use a bonus action to pull the blade’s trigger. With a pneumatic thrust, the top of the weapon arcs forward and you gain a +4 bonus to the attack roll.
Tetanus Blade. When you hit a creature with an attack that uses Pneumatic Strike, the pathogens that live within the rusty blade are reinvigorated by its magic, and the attack deals an additional 4 (1d8) Poison damage.Backfire. When you roll an 8 on Tetanus Blade’s poison damage, dormant pathogens within surrounding creatures become reinvigorated. Each creature within 10 feet of you (including you) must succeed on a DC 15 Constitution saving throw or take 14 (4d6) Poison damage and become poisoned until the end of its next turn.

You sting the eyes of a creature attacking you. The target must make a Constitution saving throw (a creature with Blindsight or Immunity to the Blinded condition succeeds automatically). On a failed save, the target has the Blinded condition until the end of the turn. On a successful save, it must subtract 1d4 from the triggering attack roll. The target automatically succeeds on its saves against your subsequent casting of this spell for 24 hours.

**카구야:** True Strike 예지계
Guided by a flash of magical insight, you make one attack with the weapon used in the spell’s casting. The attack uses your spellcasting ability for the attack and damage rolls instead of using Strength or Dexterity. If the attack deals damage, it can be Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type (your choice). Cantrip Upgrade. Whether you deal Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type, the attack deals extra Radiant damage when you reach levels 5 (1d6), 11 (2d6), and 17 (3d6).

**카구야:** Longbow of Melodies 군용 원거리 무기 • Slow
This bow has multiple strings and resembles a lyre or small harp. By strumming the strings while setting an arrow to the bow, you imbue the arrow with magic. You can play one of the following melodies when you use the bow to make a ranged weapon attack. You must choose to do so before you make the attack roll, and you can play only one melody per attack. Melody of Precision. If you’re proficient in Performance, you gain a +1 bonus to the attack roll. If you have expertise in Performance, you gain a +2 bonus instead. Melody of Reverberation. The melody you strum echoes loudly. On a hit, the target takes extra thunder damage equal to your Charisma modifier.

You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. **네모(Nemo):** Sorcerous Burst Evocation
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder. If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).

You encountered something dreadful, a horrible creature or bizarre ritual that set you down the path to becoming an investigator of the strange. Your quick feet and instinct for survival carried you through that day and are your best asset. You gain the following benefits. Instinct to Survive. When you take damage that would reduce you to 0 hit points, you can immediately regain hit points equal to your level. When you use this benefit, you cannot use it again until you finish a long rest. Superior Speed. You gain a +10 bonus to speed. Wriggle Free. If you would gain the Grappled condition, roll a d20. On a 10 or higher, you instead do not gain it.

**카린츠:** Vow of Enmity Feature
When you take the Attack action, you can expend one use of your Channel Divinity to utter a vow of enmity against a creature you can see within 30 feet of yourself. You have Advantage on attack rolls against the creature for 1 minute or until you use this feature again. If the creature drops to 0 Hit Points before the vow ends, you can transfer the vow to a different creature within 30 feet of yourself (no action required).

**엘테라 마스테:** Spirit Shroud 3rd Level • Necromancy
You call forth spirits of the dead, which flit around you for the spell’s duration. The spirits are intangible and invulnerable. Until the spell ends, any attack you make deals 1d8 extra damage when you hit a creature within 10 feet of you. This damage is radiant, necrotic, or cold (your choice when you cast the spell). Any creature that takes this damage can’t regain hit points until the start of your next turn. In addition, any creature of your choice that you can see that starts its turn within 10 feet of you has its speed reduced by 10 feet until the start of your next turn. At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 4th level or higher, the damage increases by 1d8 for every two slot levels above 3rd.

**네모(Nemo):** Mirror Spell 3rd Level • Abjuration
You attempt to copy and cast a spell of level 3 or lower that you can see being cast. You can only copy spells cast by creatures, and you can’t copy your own spell. If the triggering spell is level 2 or lower, you automatically copy and cast the spell. If the spell is level 3 or higher, you must succeed on an ability check using your spellcasting ability (DC 10 plus the triggering spell’s level) to copy and cast the spell. When casting a copied spell, you don’t expend a spell slot and you don’t need any components. Treat the spell as if you were its original caster, using your own spellcasting ability modifier and save DC, and casting it at the lowest level it can be cast. Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. Treat the level of the spell slot used as the maximum level of spell you can copy and cast.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Trigger which you take when you see a creature within 60 feet of you casting a spell V, S Reaction Instantaneous 60 ft

**네모(Nemo):** Chaos Bolt 1st Level • Evocation
You hurl an undulating, warbling mass of chaotic energy at one creature in range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 2d8 + 1d6 damage. Choose one of the d8s. The number rolled on that die determines the attack’s damage type, as shown below.
d8 Damage Type 1 Acid 2 Cold 3 Fire 4 Force 5 Lightning 6 Poison 7 Psychic 8 Thunder
Open RollTable Chaos Bolt: Damage Type
If you roll the same number on both d8s, the chaotic energy leaps from the target to a different creature of your choice within 30 feet of it. Make a new attack roll against the new target, and make a new damage roll, which could cause the chaotic energy to leap again. A creature can be targeted only once by each casting of this spell. At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 2nd level or higher, each target takes 1d6 extra damage of the type rolled for each slot level above 1st.

An event in your past left an indelible mark on you, infusing you with simmering magic. As a Bonus Action, you can unleash that magic for 1 minute, during which you gain the following benefits: The spell save DC of your Sorcerer spells increases by 1. You have Advantage on the attack rolls of Sorcerer spells you cast. You can use this feature twice, and you regain all expended uses of it when you finish a Long Rest.

**매그너스:** Rage Feature
You can imbue yourself with a primal power called Rage, a force that grants you extraordinary might and resilience. You can enter it as a Bonus Action if you aren’t wearing Heavy armor. You can enter your Rage the number of times shown for your Barbarian level in the Rages column of the Barbarian Features table. You regain one expended use when you finish a Short Rest, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. While active, your Rage follows the rules below. Damage Resistance. You have Resistance to Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing damage. Rage Damage. When you make an attack using Strength—with either a weapon or an Unarmed Strike—and deal damage to the target, you gain a bonus to the damage that increases as you gain levels as a Barbarian, as shown in the Rage Damage column of the Barbarian Features table. Strength Advantage. You have Advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. No Concentration or Spells. You can’t maintain Concentration, and you can’t cast spells. Duration. The Rage lasts until the end of your next turn, and it ends early if you don Heavy armor or have the Incapacitated condition. If your Rage is still active on your next turn, you can extend the Rage for another round by doing one of the following: Make an attack roll against an enemy. Force an enemy to make a saving throw. Take a Bonus Action to extend your Rage. Each time the Rage is extended, it lasts until the end of your next turn. You can maintain a Rage for up to 10 minutes.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Bonus Action 10 minutes Self Self

**매그너스:** Unarmed Strike Simple Melee
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick, head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a target within 5 feet of you.Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for its effect.Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier. Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you and if you have a hand free to grab it. Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you.
Action Instantaneous 1 creature Equipped Proficient

**매그너스:** Unarmed Strike Simple Melee
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick, head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a target within 5 feet of you.Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for its effect.Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier. Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you and if you have a hand free to grab it. Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you.

**카구야:** @볼을 부풀리고 불만 가득한 표정이지만 뭐라 말은 하지 않습니다.

**Gamemaster:** 후일담

**Gamemaster:** 일행이 밤늦게 오리진으로 복귀하자 이브와 렐은 감격의 재회를 했습니다.

**Gamemaster:** 재회가 끝나자 이브는 여러분들의 이야기를 경청하곤 그런 일이 있었을 줄은 몰랐다며 여러분의 안위를 살폈습니다.

**Gamemaster:** 그리고 그 고생에 비하면 얼마 안되겠지만 자신의 고향을 떠나올때 받은 봇짐을 모두 일행에게 전달했죠.

**Gamemaster:** 과연 그 봇짐에 무엇이 들어있을지는 돌아가서 확인해봐야겠군요

**Gamemaster:** 수고하셨슴미당

**엘테라 마스테:** 쿠오옷…수고 많으셨습니다

**Gamemaster:** 후 길어졌다

**헤카트리엘:** 슈고~

**네모(Nemo):** 고생하셨습니다

**카구야:** 수고하셨어용

**네모(Nemo):** 하 실수해버렸네 쩝

**카린츠:** 슈공~

My job here is mostly to keep this module maintained and working on Foundry v11 and future updates. That said I am not opposed to expanding this module with additional systems or new features if there is big demand enough.</p> <p class="nue">Since I took this module with next to no knowledge, keep in mind that I might not know if something is broken or not working as intended. Please feel free to contact me on Foundry Discord by pinging Forien.
